  "content": {
    "tool_use_id": "toolu_015pqASWUrYFyfcx81gfP1iA",
    "type": "tool_result",
    "content": "  /**\n   * Called when a character arrives at the tile adjacent to their talk target.\n   * Checks proximity and re-evaluates B's availability before starting conversation.\n   */\n  _handleTalkArrival(char) {\n    const target = char.pendingTalkTarget;\n    char.pendingTalkTarget = null;\n\n    // Proximity check: target may have moved significantly during the walk.\n    const dx   = Math.round(target.tx) - Math.round(char.tx);\n    const dy   = Math.round(target.ty) - Math.round(char.ty);\n    const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);\n\n    if (dist > 3) {\n      // Target has drifted \u2014 try to follow if not too far\n      if (dist <= 10) {\n        const adjTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));\n        if (adjTile && char.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {\n          // Re-attach pending talk so we retry on next arrival\n          char.pendingTalkTarget   = target;\n          char._talkRetargetTimer  = 2000;\n          return;\n        }\n      }\n      // Too far or unreachable \u2014 abort\n      this.pendingEvents.push({\n        type:      'fallback',\n        charLabel: char.label,\n        reason:    'talk_target_moved',\n        fromLabel: target.label,\n        toLabel:   null,\n      });\n      char.pendingTalkDialogue = null;\n      char.pendingTalkResponse = null;\n      char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Re-check availability: accept if idle or walking, reject if busy\n    const canTalk = target.action === 'idle' || target.action === 'walking';\n\n    if (!canTalk) {\n      this.pendingEvents.push({\n        type:           'talk_rejected',\n        initiatorLabel: char.label,\n        targetLabel:    target.label,\n      });\n      char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;\n      return;\n    }\n\n    this._startConversation(char, target);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Configurable conversation duration range (ms).\n   * Defaults to 10\u201315 s; override via constructor config.\n   */\n  get _talkDurationMs() {\n    return 10_000 + Math.random() * 5_000;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Synchronise charA and charB into a shared 'talking' state.\n   * Both face each other, AI timers are paused (via action check in AIEngine),\n   * and conversation ends naturally when the timer expires.\n   */\n  _startConversation(charA, charB) {\n    const duration = this._talkDurationMs;",

{"id":"798bfe70-164b-498e-a578-109b2e24c5ec","identifier":"FRG-224","title":"Fallback Logic (Plan B / Re-evaluation)","description":"Characters need re-evaluation triggers when their plan becomes invalid mid-execution.

## Current Problem

Once a character decides on an action, they commit fully. If the target object gets occupied while walking, or the character they wanted to talk to moves away, they continue anyway — leading to nonsensical behavior.

## Requirements

1. **Target Occupied:** If walking to an object and it becomes full before arrival → pick next closest available object of similar type, or fall back to idle.
2. **Target Moved:** If walking to talk to a character and they move away → update destination every few seconds, or abort if too far.
3. **Path Blocked:** If path becomes blocked → wait briefly and retry, or pick alternative destination.
4. **Blackboard Pattern:** Shared state where characters post intentions. Other characters can check before committing (e.g., 'Maple is heading to the stove' → Sol picks a different object).

## Acceptance Criteria

* Characters abort interactions when target becomes unavailable
* Characters pick alternatives instead of getting stuck
* Intent broadcasting prevents multiple characters targeting the same object
* Debug page shows character intentions/targets
* Event log shows fallback decisions (e.g., 'stove busy, chose bookshelf instead')","projectMilestone":{"id":"d98e487a-66f2-4106-86d3-550aac4cb898","name":"M1: Sim engine correct (debug foundation)"},"priority":{"value":2,"name":"High"},"url":"https://linear.app/chills-linear/issue/FRG-224/fallback-logic-plan-b-re-evaluation","gitBranchName":"chillkimtest/frg-224-fallback-logic-plan-b-re-evaluation","createdAt":"2026-03-07T17:41:11.854Z","updatedAt":"2026-03-07T18:19:36.412Z","archivedAt":null,"completedAt":null,"dueDate":null,"slaStartedAt":null,"slaMediumRiskAt":null,"slaHighRiskAt":null,"slaBreachesAt":null,"slaType":"all","status":"Test in Progress","labels":[],"attachments":[{"id":"cbc3a57c-f1ab-45ac-b382-ca3745a05271","title":"feat: fallback logic and plan re-evaluation (FRG-224)","subtitle":null,"url":"https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/ai-aquarium-phaser/pull/10"}],"documents":[],"createdBy":"Chill","createdById":"b5a6e03a-2da1-4e78-951b-81497e2a00f7","assignee":"Chill","assigneeId":"b5a6e03a-2da1-4e78-951b-81497e2a00f7","project":"AI Aquarium","projectId":"0385a8c7-ba5a-43a3-b223-acf4d1ad6d63","team":"Forge","teamId":"c3ef97d8-21a8-4aa7-a818-298f217864dd"}

## Status DONE ## What Changed - **`src/objects.js`** — added `getReservations()` and `getOccupants()` public methods to `ObjectInstance` so the debug UI and AI engine can read slot intent by character name - **`src/Character.js`** — added `_talkRetargetTimer` field to support periodic talk-route recalculation - **`src/Engine.js`** — multiple changes: - `_handleObjectArrival`: clears targeting before interaction; on failure calls `_fallbackToAlternativeObject` instead of silently idling - `_handleTalkArrival`: proximity check (> 3 tiles → re-follow, > 10 tiles → abort) before starting a conversation - `_doWander`: skips objects whose current state has no `use` transition - Added `_findAlternativeObject`, `_fallbackToAlternativeObject`, `_updateTalkRoute` helpers - `update()` loop: ticks `_talkRetargetTimer` and calls `_updateTalkRoute` every 2 s while walking to a talk target - **`src/AIEngine.js`** — `_requestDecision`: adds `intendedBy`/`usedBy` fields to the objects prompt (blackboard); `_applyDecision`: guards the `interact` case with a usability check and verifies `reserve()` succeeds - **`debug.html`** — fallback CSS + log rendering (amber `FALLBACK` tag), slot pips now show character name tooltips, character intent labels include status suffixes (`reserved`, `following`, `using`), event loop now also consumes `fallback` events ## Key Decisions - **Fallback finds nearest alternative by Euclidean distance** (not same type) — the codebase has no object type taxonomy, and nearest-available is the most sensible behaviour - **Talk abort threshold = 10 tiles** — gives enough room for normal character wandering while still aborting if a target is clearly unreachable - **Route recheck every 2 s** — balances responsiveness vs. path-find cost; characters typically move < 1 tile/s so this is sufficient ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feature/FRG-224-fallback-logic-re-evaluation` - PR: https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/ai-aquarium-phaser/pull/10
